## 321 Chad/Libya V (1981-1981)  {.tabset}

informal, or tacit.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b0c3c4b"><p class="cl-9b0c185a"><span class="cl-9b0c0d38">Mozambique</span><span class="cl-9b0c0d24"> </span><span neighbors.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b28b6d6"><p class="cl-9b288de6"><span class="cl-9b2882ce">No</span><span class="cl-9b2882ce"> </span><span class="cl-9b2882ce">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr attributed the loss to its planes being "blown over the border by adverse winds."In early April 1981 the Reagan administration cut off U.S. aid to the new regime in Nicaragua.</span></p></td><td down two Syrian helicopters carrying supplies to Syrian troops on Mount Sanin overlooking Zahle.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b30ed38"><p class="cl-9b30c542"><span class="cl-9b30b962">Israel</span><span class="cl-9b30b94e"> </span><span class="cl-9b30b94e">initiated</span><span class="cl-9b30b94e"> </span><span class="cl-9b30b962">attack</span><span each other of violating the 1976 Red Line agreement: by the use of Syrian air power against any party to the civil war and the introduction of missiles into Lebanon; and by Israel's intervention in the civil war with air power far north of the Israel/Lebanon border.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b30ed38"><p class="cl-9b30c542"><span class="cl-9b30b962">Israel</span><span class="cl-9b30b94e"> agreement in the Cameroonian town of Maroua: the access channel to the port of Calabar was to remain within Nigeria's territorial waters; and the rights of Nigerian fishers within a two-kilometer goal, Angolan army headquarters in Xangongo had also been heavily bombed.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b5529de"><p class="cl-9b550042"><span class="cl-9b54f4ee">No</span><span class="cl-9b54f4ee"> </span><span class="cl-9b54f4ee">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9b5529dc"><p class="cl-9b550042"><span class="cl-9b54f4ee">331.13</span></p></td><td African forces from Angola.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b5529d2"><p class="cl-9b550042"><span class="cl-9b54f4f8">United</span><span class="cl-9b54f4f8"> </span><span research defense agency inspect the submarine, for nuclear material was suspected.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b69e8cc"><p class="cl-9b69b65e"><span class="cl-9b69ab32">Sweden</span><span class="cl-9b69b65e"><span class="cl-9b69ab28">That cluster of decisions triggered a crisis for the USSR. Moscow perceived a multifaceted threat: to its superpower image; to its influence among nonaligned states; to its relations with Sweden; and to its image for probity regarding nuclear material.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b69e8c2"><p class="cl-9b69b65e"><span class="cl-9b69ab32">Soviet</span><span class="cl-9b69ab32"> </span><span class="cl-9b69ab32">Union</span><span class="cl-9b69ab32">start</span><span class="cl-9b69ab32"> </span><span class="cl-9b69ab32">of</span><span class="cl-9b69ab32"> </span><span class="cl-9b69ab32">crisis</span><span class="cl-9b69ab28"> </span><span class="cl-9b69ab28">about</span><span class="cl-9b69ab28"> </span><span class="cl-9b69ab32">sentence</span><span class="cl-9b69ab32"> </span><span class="cl-9b69ab32">6</span><span class="cl-9b69ab28">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9b69e8cd"><p class="cl-9b69b65e"><span class="cl-9b69ab28">333.8</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b69e8cc"><p class="cl-9b69b65e"><span class="cl-9b69ab28">At a meeting of Sweden's crisis group on the 29th preparations were made for possible violence in the Karlskrona area.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b69e8cc"><p class="cl-9b69b65e"><span class="cl-9b69ab28">No</span><span class="cl-9b69ab28"> </span><span class="cl-9b69ab28">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr same day that Sweden had the right to question the submarine commander, to investigate the incident, and to conduct rescue operations.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b69e8cc"><p class="cl-9b69e8c2"><p class="cl-9b69b65e"><span class="cl-9b69ab28">No</span><span class="cl-9b69ab28"> </span><span class="cl-9b69ab28">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr class="cl-9b69ab28">The UN and the U.S. were not involved in this crisis.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b69e8cc"><p class="cl-9b69b65e"><span class="cl-9b69ab28">No</span><span class="cl-9b69ab28"> </span><span class="cl-9b69ab28">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9b69e8ce"><p class="cl-9b69b65e"><span class="cl-9b69ab28">333.29</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b69e8d6"><p class="cl-9b69b65e"><span class="cl-9b69ab28">(In February 1995, Sweden's premier confirmed that most intrusions into its territorial waters during the preceding 20 years were minks -- which generated sound patterns similar to those of submarines -- not Soviet subs!)</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b69e8d6"><p class="cl-9b69b65e"><span class="cl-9b69ab28">No</span><span class="cl-9b69ab28"> </span><span class="cl-9b69ab28">events.</span></p></td></tr></tbody></table></div>

class="cl-9b71fcba">334.1</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fc8"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">Bahrain and Sa'udi Arabia experienced a crisis with Iran from 13 December 1981 to 8 January 1982.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fc8"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">No</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b722fdc"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">BackgroundBahrain is a tiny oil-rich Gulf sheikhdom, comprising 33 islands between the Qatar Peninsula and the Sa'udi Arabian coast.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fdc"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">No</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9b722fd2"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">334.3</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fc8"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">It has an area of 230 square miles and a population of less than half a million, half of whom are foreigners.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fc8"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">No</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9b722fdd"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">334.4</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fdc"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">Bahrain was a U.K. protectorate from 1861, formally since 1880, to 1971.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fdc"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">No</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9b722fd2"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">334.5</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fc8"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">London's announcement in 1968 that it would end the protectorate and withdraw British forces from the Gulf in 1971 led Iran to revive its long-standing claim to sovereignty over Bahrain, as part of its goal of hegemony in the Gulf.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fc8"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">United</span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">Kingdom</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">initiated</span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">Bahrain</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">.</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">Iran</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span having ruled the island from 1753 to 1783.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fdc"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">No</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9b722fd2"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">334.7</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fc8"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">Like all the small Gulf sheikhdoms, which became independent following the U.K.'s further retreat from empire, Bahrain was vulnerable to encroachments from the three competing major powers in the region, Iran, Iraq, and Sa'udi Arabia.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fc8"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">No</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9b722fdd"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">334.8</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fdc"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">Two upheavals nearby heightened Bahrain's sense of insecurity from external and internal sources: the fall of the shah and the emergence of an Islamic revolutionary regime under the leadership of Ayatullah Khomeini in 1979; and the outbreak of a war between Iran and Iraq in September 1980.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fdc"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">No</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9b722fd2"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">334.9</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fc8"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">As that war dragged on, the increasingly audible messianic fervor of Iran's fundamentalist regime generated more intense fear among the Gulf sheikhdoms.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fc8"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">No</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9b722fdd"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">334.10</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fdc"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">On 13 December 1981 Bahrain's Interior Ministry announced the arrest of a group of Bahrainis and other Gulf nationals accused of trying to overthrow the regime: their attempted coup triggered a crisis for the island-state.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fdc"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span plot.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fc8"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">Bahrain</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">initiated</span><span to Sa'udi Arabia and all Gulf states: the course of the Iran/Iraq War and the danger of an Iranian victory raised serious Sa'udi concerns about Iraq's ability to withstand the onslaught and the consequences of an Iranian triumph for the Sa'udi regime.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fdc"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">Saudi</span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4"> </span><span class="cl-9b722fdc"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">Two months later, Sa'udi Arabia strengthened its hegemony among the Gulf states by signing similar agreements with three other members of the Gulf Cooperation Council, which was established that year -- Oman, Qatar, and the United Arab Emirates.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fdc"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">Saudi</span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">Arabia</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">initiated</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">mutual</span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">defense</span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">pact</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">toward</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">Oman;Qatar;United</span><span style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9b722fd2"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">334.17</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fc8"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcba">Crisis termination for Bahrain can be dated as 8 January 1982: that day, bolstered by the security agreement with Sa'udi Arabia and implied support from Iran's most powerful foe, the United States, to which Bahrain had granted a de facto naval base in the 1970s, Bahrain banned Iranians from the sheikhdom, suspended economic relations with Iran, and declared martial law.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9b722fc8"><p class="cl-9b72085e"><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">Bahrain</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">initiated</span><span </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">experienced</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">a</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">end</span><span </span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">this</span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4"> </span><span class="cl-9b71fcc4">sentence</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba">.</span><span class="cl-9b71fcba"> </span><span
